[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m[1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpanderFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:52[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: 7bb3f9683ba8f59b[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA critical security issue was detected by Jazzer’s FilePathTraversal sanitizer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzz testing of the Apache Commons Compress Expander example. The fuzzer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput caused a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception indicating a file path [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal vulnerability when expanding archive entries. The error originates in the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FilePathTraversal.check` logic and propagates through the `Expander.expand` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethods invoked by the fuzzer harness.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzzing, a specially crafted input triggered a [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception. This indicates that an archive entry’s path escapes the intended [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction directory, allowing for potential overwriting or creation of files [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutside the target directory.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  File path traversal: unvalidated or improperly sanitized file paths in archive [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction can lead to writing files to arbitrary locations.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Observations and Findings  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception stack trace shows the failure occurs in [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFilePathTraversal.check[0m[1;39m([0m[39mFilePathTraversal.jav[0m[1;92ma:346[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The call chain:  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `FilePathTraversal.checkPath` → `FilePathTraversal.copyMismatchMvHook` →  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      `Expander.expand` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmultiple overloads[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sanitizer detected that the normalized output path [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/tmp/[0m[39m…[0m[35m/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m navigates outside the intended extraction root.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • A crashing input was deduplicated with token `7bb3f9683ba8f59b`, demonstrating [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreproducibility of the path traversal condition.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m merely drives the API under test and is not the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot cause; it loads the input and calls `Expander.expand`.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal`  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Methods `check`, `checkPath`, and `copyMismatchMvHook` for path [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalization and validation logic.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander` class  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – All overloads of the `expand` method handling archive entry names and output[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile paths.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Entry point that feeds the malicious input to the `Expander` API; useful for[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreproducing the issue but not the source of the vulnerability.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHere is the initial issue log of the codebase:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<issue>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== Java Exception: com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Analyze root cause and critical logic[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The exception arises when `Expander` attempts to resolve or write archive [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries whose names include path traversal patterns [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., “…[0m[35m/[0m[39m”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Internally, calls[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuch as `[0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or manual [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` throw an `IOException` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor trigger[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer’s FilePathTraversal sanitizer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when the resulting path escapes the intended [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`targetDirectory`.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Two code paths must be patched:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m The generic `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mArchiveEntrySupplier<T>, ArchiveEntryBiConsumer<T>, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m68[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m76[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m The ZIP‐specific `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mZipFile, Path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m480[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m500[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must preserve:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Extraction of valid entries [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfiles, directories, symlinks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Existing directory‐creation and data–copy logic.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • The public API signatures and behavior for legitimate archives.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must **not** modify the fuzzer harness, utility functions, or test code.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy to safely ignore traversal attempts[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Patch the generic entry‐loop:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Surround the `resolveIn` call in a try/catch that catches `IOException`.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - On catching an `IOException` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mindicative of zip‐slip/traversal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, log a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwarning and **skip** that entry by continuing the loop.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This prevents the exception from bubbling up to Jazzer’s sanitizer while [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill processing further entries.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Example pseudocode change at `Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:68[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m76[0m[39m`:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            final Path targetPath;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                targetPath = nullTarget[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                    ? null[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                    : [0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIOException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Detected path‐traversal; skip this entry[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mLOGGER.warn[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Skipping illegal entry path: [0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m"[0m[39m, [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnextEntry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                nextEntry = [0m[1;35msupplier.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                continue;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m existing logic to create directories [0m[35m/[0m[39m write files [0m[35m/[0m[39m symlinks[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            …[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            nextEntry = [0m[1;35msupplier.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Patch the ZIP‐specific loop:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace the hard `throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip…"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` guard with a skip.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Before creating or copying the file, check [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mnormalizedTarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. If false, log and `continue`.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - For symlink entries, also verify both the link path and the symlink target [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdo not escape `targetDirectory`. If they do, skip the entry.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Example pseudocode change around `Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:490[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m500[0m[39m`:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        Path candidate = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m! [0m[1;35mcandidate.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mLOGGER.warn[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Skipping zip entry outside target: [0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m"[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            continue;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m proceed to create parent dirs and copy data[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `Expander.java` and locate the generic expand method [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`<T extends [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mArchiveEntry>` around line [0m[1;36m68[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Insert try/catch around `[0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` as described.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the ZIP‐specific `while [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mentries.hasMoreElements[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` block [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maround lines [0m[1;36m475[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m505[0m[39m.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Change the two‐line check that currently throws an `IOException` into a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguard that logs and `continue`s.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Add analogous checks for symlink creation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mensure both link and target stay[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder `targetDirectory`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Add a logger [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., using `org.slf4j.LoggerFactory`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at the top of `Expander`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif not already present, to replace `System.err`.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Compile and run existing unit tests; ensure no regressions occur.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Re-run the Jazzer fuzzer harness; verify that traversal‐triggering inputs are[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnow skipped instead of crashing.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By catching the specific `IOException` thrown during path resolution, we [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevent malicious entries from aborting the entire extraction process.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Skipping only the offending entries preserves extraction of all legitimate [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach maintains public API behavior: valid archives still expand [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfully, and invalid paths are simply ignored with a warning.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to fuzz harness, utility classes, or external dependencies—only the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcore extraction logic in `Expander`.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential side effects and mitigation[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Side effect: Malicious entries will be silently omitted. However, this is the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesired hardening—no arbitrary files are written outside the target directory.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: The user will see a warning in logs for skipped entries. If strict[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfeedback is required, one could collect skipped entries into a user‐accessible list[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor throw an `ArchiveException` after processing, but that is out of scope for [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving existing functionality.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing tests and valid use cases remain unaffected.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.j[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mav[0m[1;92ma:68[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m76[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.j[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mav[0m[1;92ma:480[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m500[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer detected a critical file path traversal vulnerability when expanding [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchives in the `Expander` example class. In response, a patch was proposed that:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Added Java logging [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`Logger`, `Level`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at the top of `Expander.java`[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Wrapped calls to `[0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in a try/catch, logging and skipping [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon failure[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Normalized and bounds-checked symlink and regular entries, logging instead of [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrowing on out-of-bounds paths[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying the patch, the build fails with multiple compilation errors: calls [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` no longer match any existing overloads, and the newly referenced [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LOGGER` symbol cannot be resolved.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The fuzzer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJazzer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m triggered a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal` exception when `Expander.expand` attempted to write unpacked archive [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries under a malicious or crafted path. The stack trace pinpointed:[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `FilePathTraversal.check` in the Jazzer sanitizer  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Multiple invocations of `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Observations in the Initial Issue  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The traversal detection occurs in commons-compress example code, not in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproduction logic.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerable code path combines `[0m[1;35msupplier.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, and subsequent file or symlink operations [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout adequate sanitization or normalization.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The failure is reproducible by the fuzzer delivering a crafted archive that [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mescapes `targetDirectory`.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Changes introduced in `Expander.java`:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Imports  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      + `import java.util.logging.Logger;`  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      + `import java.util.logging.Level;`[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Logger Declaration  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      + Inserted inside the class:  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        `private static final Logger LOGGER = [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mLogger.getLogger[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mExpander.class.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Entry Path Resolution  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Wrapping `[0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in try/catch  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - On `IOException`, log warning and skip entry  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Symlink Handling  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Normalized both link and target paths  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Logged and continued on any path outside `targetDirectory`  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Zip Slip Check for Regular Files  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Normalized the target path  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Logged and skipped entries that resolve outside the intended directory  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Patch Application Log  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The compiler reports five errors in `Expander.java`:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Method Signature Mismatches [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthree locations: lines ~[0m[1;36m141[0m[39m, ~[0m[1;36m254[0m[39m, ~[0m[1;36m458[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Calls like `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m -> [0m[1;39m{[0m[33m...[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry, out[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m -> [0m[1;39m{[0m[33m...[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m, targetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` no [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlonger match any `expand` overload.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Existing overloads expect `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream, File, CloseableConsumer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString, Path, Path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, none accept functional interfaces `ArchiveEntrySupplier` or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ArchiveEntryBiConsumer`.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Undefined Symbol `LOGGER` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtwo locations: lines ~[0m[1;36m497[0m[39m, ~[0m[1;36m511[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - References to `LOGGER` cannot be found, indicating the `LOGGER` field [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meither wasn’t placed in the correct class scope or the import/field insertion was [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmisplaced.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Code Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The set of existing `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` overloads and their exact parameter types in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander.java`  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Import statements and class visibility: verify that `java.util.logging.Logger`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `Level` imports are at the correct top-of-file scope  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All call sites of `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in `Expander.java` to ensure they reference [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe correct overload or are refactored to use the new one[0m                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Restore correct placement of the `public class Expander` declaration and ensure [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma single, top‐level class definition.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the erroneously inserted `public class Expander [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` line that appears [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately before the generic `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mArchiveEntrySupplier<T>, [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mArchiveEntryBiConsumer<T>, Path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method. This duplicate class declaration is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshadowing the file’s real class scope and preventing the static `LOGGER` field from[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeing visible.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Relocate the `LOGGER` declaration into the top‐level class body, directly [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeneath the existing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand only[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m `public class Expander [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` line:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After the class Javadoc [0m[1;39m([0m[39mending around line [0m[1;36m50[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the line `public class [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mExpander [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m`, insert:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private static final java.util.logging.Logger LOGGER =[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mjava.util.logging.Logger.getLogger[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mExpander.class.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures that `LOGGER` is in class scope and resolvable from all methods.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Move the two `import` statements for Java logging into the imports section at [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe top of the file, alongside the other `java.*` imports:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   import java.util.logging.Logger;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   import java.util.logging.Level;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This guarantees that `Logger` and `Level` types are recognized by the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompiler.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Verify that the private generic method signature remains unchanged:[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   private <T extends ArchiveEntry>[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   void [0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mArchiveEntrySupplier<T> supplier,[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               ArchiveEntryBiConsumer<T> writer,[0m                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvisible within the class.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
